# pornographic search engines for the domain names in the search results, as well as 
#   manually adding domains during blocklist verification.

# When using many other blocklists from various sources, I find them lacking in certain areas.
# This was created in an attempt to put on the finishing touches and try to acheive exhautstive blockage
#
# I have only tested this with pfBlockerNG in pfSense, but im trying to follow the same formating
#   I've seen in most other blocklists for various usage.
#
# I haven't decided if I want to release the scraping library yet.
#
# If you notice any domains that were missed and would like me to add them to this list, please email or message me
#   and I will add them to the manual blocklist. 
#
# If you notice any false alarms and would like me to add them to the perminent whitelist, please do notify me, as any
#   help maintaining an accurate and effective list is much welcome.
#
# Note to self: To get pfBlockerNG to re-download the blocklist on forced run, first remove 
#   the file "Pr0nBlocklist.txt" in pfSense like so: rm /var/db/pfblockerng/dnsbl/Pr0nBlocklist.txt
